<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>**Hook:** &quotWrong timing?&quot</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>**CTA:** Not interested / Remind me Q2</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>## ‚úÖ Pre-Launch Checklist (High-Level)</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>## üìä Expected Results</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### Conservative Scenario (Good Campaign)</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- 10% reply rate ‚Üí **9 replies**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- 8% meeting booked ‚Üí **7 meetings**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- 75% show rate ‚Üí **5 meetings held**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- 20% conversion ‚Üí **1 opportunity**</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- 10% meeting booked ‚Üí **9 meetings**</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>## üí° Pro Tips for Maximum Success</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### 1. **Invest in Personalization Research**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>The difference between 3% and 18% reply rates is the quality of Column 9 data. Spend the 5-6 hours doing proper research.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### 2. **Test First, Then Scale**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>Send to 20 contacts first. Learn what works. Apply those learnings to the remaining 73.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### 3. **Respond Fast**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>Reply within 2 hours. Speed wins in sales. Have response templates ready.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### 4. **Track Everything**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>Use the daily tracking table. Data from this campaign informs the next one.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### 5. **Be Human**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>These are peers. Sales leader to sales leader. Be authentic, helpful, and direct.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>---</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>## üéØ Campaign Philosophy</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>&gt **&quotWe're not pitching. We're showing sales leaders a better way to work.&quot**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>This campaign isn't about manipulation or tricks. It's about:</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Solving real problems (prioritization crisis)</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Offering genuine value (Signal + Execution)</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Being helpful and authentic</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Respecting their time and intelligence</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>If they see the value, they'll want to talk.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>If they don't, we move on respectfully.</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>**Quality conversations &gt Quantity of sends**</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>---</tt></span></font></div>

<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>## üìà Success Benchmarks</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### Day 1 After First Send</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Open rate should be 55%+ within 24 hours</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- At least 1-2 replies from first 20 sends</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Zero technical issues (bounces, broken links)</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### Week 1 (After First 20)</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- Reply rate should be trending toward 10%+</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- ROI calculator getting clicks</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>- First meeting(s) booked</tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt><br></tt></span></font></div>
<div><font face="MADMOODYRegular" color="#2A453C"><span style="font-size: 42px"><tt>### Week 2 (Full Scale)</tt></span></font></div>

## # Campaign 2 Quick Reference Card

<div><b><tt># Campaign 2 Quick Reference Card</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Print this and keep it handy during the campaign**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üìä Campaign Vitals</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Metric | Target |</tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Contacts**</tt></b><tt> | 93 Sales Directors/Heads |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Duration**</tt></b><tt> | 11 days (4 touches) |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Reply Rate**</tt></b><tt> | 12-18% |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Meetings**</tt></b><tt> | 8-12 booked |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Opportunities**</tt></b><tt> | 1-2 created |</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üìß Email Schedule</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email | Day | Time | Goal | Key CTA |</tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|---|---|---|</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**1: Signal Blindness**</tt></b><tt> | 1 (Tue/Wed) | 9-10 AM | Establish credibility | 10-min demo |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**2: Differentiation**</tt></b><tt> | 4 (Thu) | 2-3 PM | Show uniqueness | ROI calculator |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**3: Social Proof**</tt></b><tt> | 8 (Tue) | 10-11 AM | Convert with story | Case study |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**4: Breakup**</tt></b><tt> | 11 (Thu) | 3-4 PM | Respectful close | Not interested / Remind later |</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üí¨ Response Quick Replies</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### ‚úÖ Positive Response</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>&quotThis looks interesting, tell me more&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚Üí Book meeting immediately with 2 time options</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### üí∞ Pricing Question</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>&quotWhat's your pricing?&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚Üí &quotDepends on team size and features. Let me show you what you'd get first, then we'll discuss investment. [Booking link]&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### ü§î &quotNot a priority&quot</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚Üí &quotFair enough. Quick question: if your team could close 25% more deals without working weekends, when WOULD that be a priority?&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### üõë &quotNot interested&quot</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚Üí &quotThanks for letting me know. I'll close your file. If anything changes, you have my info. Good luck!&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### üèÜ Competitor Objection</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>&quotWe use Outreach/SalesLoft&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚Üí &quotMost customers were too. Main difference: they work separately (30% adoption), we work in Gmail (90% adoption). Worth 10 minutes?&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üéØ Core Messaging</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Positioning</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotSignal + Execution = Sales Excellence&quot**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Key Differentiators</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>1. </tt><b><tt>**Inbox-Native**</tt></b><tt> (Gmail/Outlook, not separate platform)</tt></div>
<div><tt>2. </tt><b><tt>**Signal + Execution**</tt></b><tt> (Not just alerts, but action)</tt></div>
<div><tt>3. </tt><b><tt>**90% Adoption**</tt></b><tt> (vs 30% industry average)</tt></div>
<div><tt>4. </tt><b><tt>**Built for Sellers**</tt></b><tt> (Not managers)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Pain Points</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- Reps flying blind on 50+ accounts</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Missing buying signals</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Context-switching chaos</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Tools sitting unused</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Working evenings/weekends</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><b><tt>## ‚ö†Ô∏è Red Flags (When to Adjust)</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| If This Happens | Do This |</tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Open rate &lt 50% after 20 sends | Test new subject lines |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Reply rate &lt 8% after 30 sends | Review personalization quality |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Click rate &lt 15% after 20 sends | Test different CTAs |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Unsubscribe rate &gt 3% | Check tone/targeting |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| 3+ bounces in a row | Verify email list quality |</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üéØ Success Mantras</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotFast follow-up wins deals&quot**</tt></b><tt> - Respond within 2 hours</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotBe human, be helpful&quot**</tt></b><tt> - No robotic responses</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotQuality &gt Quantity&quot**</tt></b><tt> - Better to have 5 great conversations than 20 meh ones</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotTrack everything&quot**</tt></b><tt> - Data drives next campaign</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**&quotCelebrate wins&quot**</tt></b><tt> - Every booked meeting counts</tt></div>

## # üöÄ Campaign 2 Launch Guide

<div><b><tt># üöÄ Campaign 2 Launch Guide</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## Braintrust Lookalikes - AISDR 4-Touch Sequence</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Campaign Status:**</tt></b><tt> Ready for Launch Prep</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Target Launch Date:**</tt></b><tt> [TBD]</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Campaign Owner:**</tt></b><tt> [Your Name]</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Expected Duration:**</tt></b><tt> 11 days from first send</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Target Audience:**</tt></b><tt> 93 Sales Directors/Heads at AI/SaaS companies</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üìã Campaign Overview</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### The Big Picture</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>This is a </tt><b><tt>**hyper-personalized, sales-to-sales peer outreach campaign**</tt></b><tt> targeting 93 Sales Directors/Heads who look like successful Braintrust customers.</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Why This Will Work:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- 84.9% pure sales roles (extremely targeted)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Peer-to-peer conversation (Director ‚Üí Director)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Grounded in Mixmax Brand Kit 2025 (Signal + Execution)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Fast-paced cadence (sales leaders decide quickly)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Differentiated positioning (vs Outreach/SalesLoft)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Success Definition</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- </tt><b><tt>**12-18% reply rate**</tt></b><tt> (industry-leading for cold outreach)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- </tt><b><tt>**8-12 meetings booked**</tt></b><tt> (8-12% conversion)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> </tt><b><tt>**5-8 meetings held**</tt></b><tt> (75% show rate)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> </tt><b><tt>**1-2 opportunities created**</tt></b><tt> (25% of held meetings)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üéØ Campaign Strategy</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Core Messaging</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Positioning:**</tt></b><tt> Signal + Execution = Sales Excellence</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Key Differentiators:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>1.</tt><tt> Inbox-native (works in Gmail/Outlook, not separate platform)</tt></div>
<div><tt>2.</tt><tt> Signal + Execution combined (not just alerts, but action)</tt></div>
<div><tt>3. 90% adoption vs 30% industry average</tt></div>
<div><tt>4.</tt><tt> Built for sellers, not managers</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Pain Points We're Hitting:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- Reps flying blind on 50+ accounts (prioritization crisis)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Missing critical buying signals</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Context-switching killing productivity</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Tools they bought sitting unused (adoption problem)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Working evenings/weekends (burnout)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Tone &amp Voice</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Mixmax Brand Mix:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Smart: 35% (data-backed, credible)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Human: 30% (peer to peer, authentic)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Rebellious: 25% (challenge status quo)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Playful: 10% (not forced, natural)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Example:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå &quotOur platform provides comprehensive sales enablement solutions&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ &quotYour reps are flying blind on 50+ accounts. We fix that.&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üìÅ Campaign Assets</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Created Documents</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Document | Purpose | Location |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|---|</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**4-Touch Sequence**</tt></b><tt> | Complete email templates with subject lines | `Campaign_2_Braintrust_4Touch_Sequence.md` |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Personalization Playbook**</tt></b><tt> | Guide for researching and populating CSV Column 9 | `Personalization_Research_Playbook.md` |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**ROI Calculator Copy**</tt></b><tt> | Landing page copy for Touch 2 CTA | `ROI_Calculator_Landing_Page.md` |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| </tt><b><tt>**Launch Guide**</tt></b><tt> | This document - master campaign orchestration | `CAMPAIGN_2_LAUNCH_GUIDE.md` |</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Email Breakdown</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Email 1 (Day 1):**</tt></b><tt> &quotThe Signal Blindness Problem&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Establish peer credibility</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Surface prioritization pain</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> CTA: 10-minute demo</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Email 2 (Day 4):**</tt></b><tt> &quotHow We're Different from Outreach&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Competitive differentiation</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Comparison table</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> CTA: ROI calculator</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Email 3 (Day 8):**</tt></b><tt> &quotSocial Proof Bomb&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Customer success story</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Results-driven</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> CTA: Case study + meeting</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Email 4 (Day 11):**</tt></b><tt> &quotThe Breakup&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Permission-based close</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Respectful exit</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> CTA: Not interested / Remind me later</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## ‚úÖ Pre-Launch Checklist</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Phase 1: Data Preparation (Week Before Launch)</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**CSV Hygiene:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] All 93 contacts verified in CSV</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Email addresses validated (use email verification tool)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Duplicate contacts removed</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Company names standardized</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Job titles clean and accurate</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Personalization Research:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Column 9 populated for all 93 contacts (use Personalization Playbook)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Trigger events recent (last 90 days)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Backup generic hooks for prospects with no news</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Quality spot-check on 10 random samples</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Team reviewed for accuracy</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Data Fields Required:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 1: First Name</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 2: Last Name</tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 3: Email</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 4: Company</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 5: Job Title</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 6: LinkedIn URL</tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 7: Company Website</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 8: [Reserved]</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 9: Personalization Info (trigger events)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Column 10: Industry (for similar company matching)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Phase 2: Technical Setup</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Sequence created: `[AISDR] Braintrust Lookalikes - Sales Director 4-Touch`</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] All 4 emails loaded into sequence</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Subject line A/B tests configured (33/33/33 split)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Send timing optimized (see schedule below)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Smart Send enabled</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Merge tags tested with sample contact</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Mobile rendering checked</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Automation Rules:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Auto-exit on reply configured</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Auto-exit on meeting booked configured</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Email opened 3+ times ‚Üí Create high-priority task</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Link clicked ‚Üí Create engagement task</tt></div>
<div><tt>- [ ] Bounced email ‚Üí Flag for cleanup</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Salesforce Integration:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Lead source tracking configured</tt></div>

<div><b><tt>## üìÖ Launch Schedule</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Week 1: Soft Launch (Testing Phase)</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 1 (Tuesday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Launch Email 1 to first 20 contacts (control group)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Send time: 9:00-10:00 AM local time (use Smart Send)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Monitor: Open rates, click rates, bounces</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 2-3 (Wednesday-Thursday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Review Email 1 performance</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Check for bounces, unsubscribes, replies</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Adjust if needed (subject lines, timing, copy)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 4 (Thursday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Email 2 sends to control group</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Send time: 2:00-3:00 PM local time</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Monitor: ROI calculator completion, replies</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 5-7 (Friday-Sunday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Review first 20 performance</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Calculate reply rate, engagement rate</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Document learnings</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Prepare for full scale</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Week 2: Full Scale Launch</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 8 (Tuesday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Launch Email 1 to remaining 73 contacts</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Apply winning subject line from control group</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Monitor metrics in real-time</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 11 (Thursday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Email 2 sends to main group</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Continue monitoring engagement</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Week 3: Optimization</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 15 (Tuesday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Email 3 sends to non-responders</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Social proof focus</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Day 18 (Thursday):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Email 4 sends to final non-responders</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Clean exit, door-open for future</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Week 4: Analysis</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><b><tt>## üìä Success Tracking</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Real-Time Metrics Dashboard</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Track Daily:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Email Performance:</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Open Rate (Target: 60%+)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Click Rate (Target: 25%+)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Reply Rate (Target: 12-18%)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îî‚îÄ Unsubscribe Rate (Keep below 2%)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Conversion Metrics:</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ ROI Calculator Completions</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Meetings Booked (Target: 8-12)</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Meetings Held (Target: 6-9)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îî‚îÄ Opportunities Created (Target: 1-2)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>By Email Performance:</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Email 1: Highest opens (establish credibility)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Email 2: Highest clicks (ROI calculator irresistible)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Email 3: Highest conversions (social proof wins)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îî‚îÄ Email 4: Clean exit (respectful close)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>A/B Test Winners:</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Subject Line Performance</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îú‚îÄ Send Time Optimization</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚îî‚îÄ CTA Button Effectiveness</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><b><tt>## üîÑ Response Handling Playbook</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Common Responses &amp How to Handle</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Positive Responses:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Response:**</tt></b><tt> &quotThis looks interesting, tell me more&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Action: Book meeting immediately</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Template: &quotAwesome! I'll share my screen and show you exactly how [their company] could achieve these results. I have [2 time slots] available this week. Which works better?&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Response:**</tt></b><tt> &quotSend me some info first&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Action: Send case study + booking link</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Template: &quotAbsolutely. Here's a case study from [similar company] that shows exactly how they achieved [results]. After you read it, let's chat for 15 minutes - I can show you the same playbook for [their company]. [Booking link]&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Response:**</tt></b><tt> &quotWhat's your pricing?&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Action: Don't quote pricing without demo</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Template: &quotGreat question! Pricing depends on team size and features you need. Rather than throw numbers at you, let me show you what you'd actually get, then we can discuss investment. [Booking link] - Takes 15 minutes.&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Objection Responses:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Objection:**</tt></b><tt> &quotWe already use Outreach/SalesLoft&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Response: &quotTotally understand. Most of our customers were using [competitor] before switching. Main difference: they work in a separate platform (30% adoption), we work in Gmail (90% adoption). Worth a 10-minute look? I can show you the side-by-side.&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Objection:**</tt></b><tt> &quotNot a priority right now&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Response: &quotFair enough, {{first_name}}. Quick question: if your team could close 25% more deals without working weekends, when WOULD that be a priority? Just trying to understand timing so I can follow up appropriately.&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Objection:**</tt></b><tt> &quotToo expensive&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Response: &quotI get it. Quick context: average customer sees ROI in 4 months from increased deals closed. If your average deal is [size] and we help close 2-3 more per quarter, does the math work? Let me show you the ROI calculator.&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Objection:**</tt></b><tt> &quotNeed to think about it&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Response: &quotAbsolutely. What specifically do you need to think about? Happy to get you any info that would help you make the decision. Is it pricing, implementation, team adoption, something else?&quot</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Negative Responses:</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Response:**</tt></b><tt> &quotNot interested&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Action: Respectful close</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Template: &quotThanks for letting me know, {{first_name}}. I'll close your file. If anything changes or you want to revisit down the road, you have my info. Good luck with [their company]!&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Response:**</tt></b><tt> &quotTake me off your list&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Action: Immediate unsubscribe + CRM update</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Template: &quotDone - you've been removed. Apologies for the inconvenience.&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üéØ Optimization Triggers</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### When to Adjust</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**If Open Rate &lt 50% after 20 sends:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Test new subject lines</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Check send timing</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Verify email deliverability</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**If Reply Rate &lt 8% after 30 sends:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Review personalization quality</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Test different pain points</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Adjust tone (more/less formal)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**If Click Rate &lt 15% after 20 sends:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Test different CTAs</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Simplify value proposition</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Add more social proof</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**If Unsubscribe Rate &gt 3%:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Review tone (too aggressive?)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Check personalization accuracy</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Verify targeting (right audience?)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üí° Pro Tips for Success</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Do's:</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ Respond to replies within 2 hours (speed matters)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ Personalize every booking request (reference their company)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ Track which personalization types perform best</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ Share winning approaches with team</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚úÖ Celebrate wins (booked meetings, great replies)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Don'ts:</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå Don't send all 93 at once (test first with 20)</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå Don't ignore bounces (clean data immediately)</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå Don't copy-paste responses (personalize replies)</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå Don't give up after one email (4-touch sequence for a reason)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚ùå Don't forget to follow up on hot leads</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt>- What underperformed</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Messaging adjustments needed</tt></div>

## # Campaign 2: Braintrust Lookalikes - 4-Touch Hyper-Personalized Sequence

<div><b><tt># Campaign 2: Braintrust Lookalikes - 4-Touch Hyper-Personalized Sequence</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Campaign Name:**</tt></b><tt> Braintrust AISDR - Sales Director Peer Outreach</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Target Audience:**</tt></b><tt> 93 Sales Directors/Heads at AI/SaaS companies</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Duration:**</tt></b><tt> 11 days</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Platform:**</tt></b><tt> AISDR (AI-powered sequencing platform)</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Brand Voice:**</tt></b><tt> Smart (35%) + Human (30%) + Rebellious (25%) + Playful (10%)</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Core Positioning:**</tt></b><tt> Signal + Execution = Sales Excellence</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**‚ö° QUICK START:**</tt></b><tt> See `AISDR_Quick_Launch_Checklist.md` for 1-2 hour deployment guide</tt></div>

<div><b><tt>## üìß EMAIL 1: The Signal Blindness Problem (Day 1)</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Send Timing:**</tt></b><tt> Tuesday/Wednesday, 9:00-10:00 AM</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Goal:**</tt></b><tt> Establish peer credibility + surface pain point</tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Primary CTA:**</tt></b><tt> 10-minute demo booking</tt></div>

<div><b><tt>### Subject Line Variants (A/B/C Test)</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Option A (Pattern Interrupt):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt>‚òë Enable Smart Send / Optimal Timing (if available in AISDR)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚òë Enable open/click tracking</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚òë A/B test subject lines (33/33/33 split)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚òë Auto-exit on reply</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>‚òë Auto-exit on meeting booked</tt></div>
<div><tt>‚òë Link to CRM if available: &quotAISDR_Braintrust_Q1&quot</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Send Schedule:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 1: Day 1 (Tue/Wed) @ 9:00-10:00 AM (recipient local time)</tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 2: Day 4 (Thu) @ 2:00-3:00 PM (recipient local time)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 3: Day 8 (Tue) @ 10:00-11:00 AM (recipient local time)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 4: Day 11 (Thu) @ 3:00-4:00 PM (recipient local time)</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Wait Times:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 1 ‚Üí Email 2: 3 days</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 2 ‚Üí Email 3: 4 days</tt></div>
<div><tt>Email 3 ‚Üí Email 4: 3 days</tt></div>
<div><tt>Total Duration: 11 days</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Automation Rules (Configure in AISDR):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Trigger | Action |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email replied | Remove from sequence immediately |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Meeting booked | Remove from sequence + alert team |</tt></div>
<div><tt>| Link clicked | Flag as engaged prospect |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email bounced | Pause for review |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Unsubscribe | Remove from all sequences |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Out of office detected | Pause sequence temporarily |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Exit Conditions:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Reply received</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Meeting booked</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Unsubscribe</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Bounced email</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Manual removal</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**üìò Detailed Setup:**</tt></b><tt> See `AISDR_Platform_Setup_Guide.md` for complete instructions</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üìä SUCCESS METRICS</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Target Benchmarks</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Overall Sequence:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Open Rate: 60%+ (sales leaders check email constantly)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Reply Rate: 12-18% (peer-to-peer conversation)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Click Rate: 25%+</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Meeting Booked Rate: 8-12%</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**By Touch:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email | Primary Metric | Target |</tt></div>
<div><tt>|---|---|---|</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email 1 | Open Rate | 65%+ |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email 2 | Click Rate (ROI calc) | 30%+ |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email 3 | Conversion Rate | 10%+ |</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>| Email 4 | Clean Exit | 5% unsubscribe max |</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**A/B Test Winners:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>- Track subject line performance after 30 sends</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Apply winning variant to remaining prospects</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Document learnings for future campaigns</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Pipeline Impact:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Meetings booked: 7-11 (8-12% of 93)</tt></div>
<div><tt>-</tt><tt> Expected show rate: 75% (5-8 meetings held)</tt></div>
<div><tt>- Expected conversion: 25% (1-2 opportunities created)</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>---</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>## üîß PERSONALIZATION VARIABLES</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>### Merge Tags to Use</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Standard Variables:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{first_name}} - First name</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{last_name}} - Last name</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{company}} - Company name</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{title}} - Job title</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{email}} - Email address</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{linkedin}} - LinkedIn URL</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Custom Variables (populate in CSV):**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{trigger_event}} - Recent company/personal news</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{similar_company_name}} - Peer company case study</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{similar_company_vertical}} - Industry match</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{similar_company_size}} - Company size match</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{similar_team_size}} - Sales team size</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{estimated_deal_size}} - Estimated average deal</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{estimated_deals_per_quarter}} - Estimated close rate</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{calculated_additional_revenue}} - 25% increase calculation</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><b><tt>**Conditional Logic:**</tt></b><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{#if_trigger_event}}</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>I saw {{trigger_event}} - congrats on the momentum.</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{/if_trigger_event}}</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt>{{#if_sales_ops_role}}</tt></div>
<div><tt>(RevOps-specific variation)</tt></div>
<div><tt>{{/if_sales_ops_role}}</tt></div>
<div><tt>```</tt><tt><br></tt></div>
<div><tt><br></tt></div>

<div><tt>-</tt><tt> [ ] Test sent to 1-2 internal emails first</tt></div>

</td><td valign="top" style="border-style: solid; border-width: 1.0px 1.0px 1.0px 1.0px; border-color: #ccc; padding: 3.0px 5.0px 3.0px 5.0px; min-width: 70px"><div>VP of Revenue Operations, Revenue Operations Manager</div>
</td></tr>
</tbody>
</table></object><br></div>
<div><b>Seniority Distribution</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>C-Level:</b>¬†25 (20.8%) ‚Üê¬†<b>HIGHEST DECISION-MAKER CONCENTRATION</b><br></li>
<li><b>Director:</b>¬†63 (52.5%)</li>
<li><b>VP:</b>¬†2 (1.7%)</li>
<li><b>Manager:</b>¬†11 (9.2%)</li>
<li><b>IC/Other:</b>¬†19 (15.8%)</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Key Characteristics</b></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Most diverse functional mix</b>¬†across all three campaigns</li>
<li><b>Highest C-level representation</b>¬†- 1 in 5 contacts is C-suite</li>
<li>Unusual for SaaS: Strong IT/Technology presence (15.8%) reflects legal industry's focus on tech infrastructure, security, and compliance</li>
<li>Operations-heavy (15.0%) - legal firms have complex operational structures</li>
<li>Lower pure sales concentration vs. typical SaaS campaigns</li>
</ol>
<div><b>Industry Context</b></div>
<div>Legal services industry shows:</div>
<ul>
<li>Technology decisions often require both business (COO/CRO) and technical (CTO/CIO) buy-in</li>
<li>Security and compliance are table-stakes</li>
<li>Strong operational governance structures</li>
<li>Partner/shareholder influence on purchasing decisions</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li><b>C-Level:</b>¬†17 (6.6%)</li>
<li><b>EVP/SVP:</b>¬†4 (1.6%)</li>
<li><b>VP:</b>¬†11 (4.3%)</li>
<li><b>Director:</b>¬†44 (17.1%)</li>
<li><b>Manager:</b>¬†29 (11.3%)</li>
<li><b>Senior (Non-Manager):</b>¬†43 (16.7%)</li>
<li><b>Individual Contributor:</b>¬†109 (42.4%) ‚Üê¬†<b>HIGHEST IC REPRESENTATION</b><br></li>
</ul>
<div><b>Key Characteristics</b></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Most balanced and diverse list</b>¬†across seniority levels</li>
<li><b>Largest dataset</b>¬†(257 contacts) - 2-3x larger than other campaigns</li>
<li><b>Highest IC representation</b>¬†(42.4%) - includes many execution-level buyers</li>
<li><b>Historical relationship</b>¬†- they know your product but chose not to continue</li>
<li>Significant Customer Success presence (8.2%) - may indicate CS-related churn</li>
</ol>
<div><b>Win-Back Context</b></div>
<div>Critical considerations:</div>
<ul>
<li><b>Loss intelligence needed:</b>¬†Why did they churn? Price? Feature gap? CS issues? Migration to competitor?</li>
<li><b>Product evolution:</b>¬†What's changed since they left?</li>
<li><b>Organizational changes:</b>¬†Are these same contacts still in same roles?</li>
<li><b>Competitive displacement:</b>¬†Which competitor won? (Critical for messaging)</li>
<li><b>Time decay:</b>¬†Q4 2024 - Q1 2025 losses = 6-12 months old (optimal win-back window)</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>GTM Sequencing Recommendations</b></div>
<div><b>Campaign 1: Legal Lookalikes - Multi-Threaded Approach</b></div>
<div><b>Recommended: 5-Touch Sequence Over 3 Weeks</b>¬†<b>Sequence Structure:</b>¬†<b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 1 (Day 1):</b>¬†C-Level Entry (COO/CRO/CEO) - 25 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotLegal ops efficiency benchmark - [Company Name]&quot</li>
<li>Angle: ROI, competitive positioning, industry-specific results</li>
<li>CTA: Executive briefing (15 min)</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 2 (Day 3):</b>¬†IT/Technology Buyers (CTO/CIO/Dir IT) - 19 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotSecurity + integration for [Company Name]&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Technical architecture, compliance, data security</li>
<li>CTA: Technical deep-dive with solutions architect</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 3 (Day 8):</b>¬†Sales/BD Directors - 31 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotHow [Similar Legal Firm] grew pipeline 43%&quot</li>
<li>Angle: User benefits, productivity gains, sales acceleration</li>
<li>CTA: Product demo focused on sales workflows</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 4 (Day 10):</b>¬†Operations Leaders - 18 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotOperational efficiency ROI for legal services&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Process optimization, cost reduction, team scaling</li>
<li>CTA: ROI calculator + case study</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 3:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 5 (Day 15):</b>¬†Multi-threaded Re-engagement</li>
<ul>
<li>Target: All non-responders from Touches 1-4</li>
<li>Format: Video message from AE/Founder</li>
<li>Angle: &quotPulling this down - last chance&quot scarcity</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Why This Works:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Legal buying involves¬†<b>multiple stakeholders</b>¬†with different concerns</li>
<li>High C-level concentration (20.8%) means executive sponsorship is achievable</li>
<li>IT/security gatekeepers must be addressed early</li>
<li>Multi-threading increases reply rate by 3-4x in enterprise deals</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Messaging Pillars by Persona:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>C-Suite:</b>¬†Industry benchmarks, competitive wins, ROI proof</li>
<li><b>IT/Tech:</b>¬†Security certifications, integration capabilities, data governance</li>
<li><b>Sales/BD:</b>¬†User experience, productivity metrics, ease of adoption</li>
<li><b>Operations:</b>¬†Cost savings, efficiency gains, team scalability</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Campaign 2: Braintrust Lookalikes - Sales-to-Sales Velocity Play</b></div>
<div><b>Recommended: 4-Touch Sequence Over 2 Weeks (Fast-Paced)</b>¬†<b>Sequence Structure:</b>¬†<b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 1 (Day 1):</b>¬†All Sales Directors/Heads - 79 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotDirector to Director: Our AiSDR approach&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Peer-to-peer conversation, sales leader pain points</li>
<li>CTA: 10-minute &quotshow me&quot demo</li>
<li>Tone: Casual, direct, sales-speak</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 2 (Day 4):</b>¬†Sales Ops/RevOps Focus - 4 contacts + relevant Directors</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotThe RevOps data you're missing&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Analytics, reporting, pipeline visibility, forecasting accuracy</li>
<li>CTA: Dashboard walkthrough</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 3 (Day 8):</b>¬†Sales Development Heads - 6 contacts + SD-focused Directors</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotSDR productivity leaderboard&quot</li>
<li>Angle: SDR/BDR efficiency, outreach volume, response rates</li>
<li>CTA: ROI calculator for SDR time savings</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 4 (Day 11):</b>¬†Breakup Email - All non-responders</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotTiming not right?&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Permission-based close, door-open for future</li>
<li>CTA: One-click &quotnot interested&quot OR &quotreach out in Q2&quot</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Why This Works:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Hyper-targeted:</b>¬†84.9% sales means everyone speaks the same language</li>
<li><b>Fast cadence:</b>¬†Sales leaders are used to quick decisions</li>
<li><b>No C-suite approval needed:</b>¬†Director-level can often trial/buy</li>
<li><b>Volume play:</b>¬†93 contacts at same level = perfect for A/B testing</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Messaging Approach:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Use¬†<b>sales metrics</b>¬†they care about: pipeline velocity, conversion rates, time-to-close</li>
<li>Include¬†<b>competitive win stories</b>¬†(if displacing manual SDR processes or other tools)</li>
<li>Show¬†<b>quick wins</b>¬†- &quotresults in first 30 days&quot</li>
<li>Leverage¬†<b>peer proof</b>¬†- &quotDirectors at [Similar Company] saw X% improvement&quot</li>
</ul>
<div><b>A/B Testing Opportunities:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Test different value props: &quotSDR productivity&quot vs &quotPipeline quality&quot vs &quotSales velocity&quot</li>
<li>Test subject lines: Question-based vs stat-based vs pattern-interrupt</li>
<li>Test CTA: Demo vs ROI calculator vs case study</li>
<li>Because everyone's at same level, clean test results</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Campaign 3: Closed Lost Win-Back - Personalized Re-Engagement</b></div>
<div><b>Recommended: 6-Touch Sequence Over 4 Weeks (Patient, Persistent)</b>¬†<b>Pre-Sequence Research Required:</b><br></div>
<ol>
<li>Pull historical data on loss reason for each account</li>
<li>Identify which competitor they moved to (if known)</li>
<li>Note any product improvements since their departure</li>
<li>Check for personnel changes (are these contacts still there?)</li>
</ol>
<div><b>Sequence Structure:</b>¬†<b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 1 (Day 1):</b>¬†CRO/VP-Level - 32 contacts (6.6% + 4.3% + 1.6%)</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotWhat's changed at [Your Company] since Q4&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Product evolution, new features, addressed pain points</li>
<li>Format: Personal video from founder/CRO</li>
<li>CTA: Executive sync (20 min)</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 1:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 2 (Day 4):</b>¬†Customer Success Managers - 21 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotHow we've transformed CS since you left&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Improved onboarding, support, customer outcomes</li>
<li>Include: CS team expansion, new resources, success metrics</li>
<li>CTA: Talk to Head of CS</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 3 (Day 8):</b>¬†Sales Directors/Managers - 73 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quot[Competitor Name] vs [Your Company] in 2025&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Competitive differentiation, feature parity, wins from their competitor</li>
<li>Include: Case study from customer who switched FROM the competitor</li>
<li>CTA: Live competitive comparison</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 2:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 4 (Day 11):</b>¬†Account Executives/ICs - 109 contacts</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotHands-on: Try the new [Product] free for 14 days&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Let them see the improvements themselves</li>
<li>CTA: Self-serve trial link OR guided demo</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 3:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 5 (Day 18):</b>¬†Multi-threaded Value Bomb</li>
<ul>
<li>Target: All non-responders</li>
<li>Format: Comprehensive &quotWhat you've missed&quot content</li>
<li>Include: Product roadmap, customer wins, industry awards, new integrations</li>
<li>CTA: Multiple CTAs based on role</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Week 4:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Touch 6 (Day 25):</b>¬†Win-Back Incentive (If Approved by Leadership)</li>
<ul>
<li>Subject: &quotWin-back offer: [Specific Incentive]&quot</li>
<li>Angle: Special pricing, extended trial, dedicated CSM, migration assistance</li>
<li>Create urgency: Limited-time offer (30 days)</li>
<li>CTA: Book win-back call with AE</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Critical Success Factors:</b><br></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Segmentation by Loss Reason:</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Price-sensitive losses: Lead with ROI + flexible pricing</li>
<li>Feature gap losses: Showcase new features that address gaps</li>
<li>CS/Support losses: Highlight CS improvements first</li>
<li>Competitive displacement: Emphasize differentiation</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Personalization Requirements:</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Reference their previous usage (if data available)</li>
<li>Acknowledge the breakup: &quotWe know you tried us in [timeframe]&quot</li>
<li>Show you've listened: &quotYou mentioned [pain point] - here's how we've addressed it&quot</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Special Considerations:</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li><b>Data quality check:</b>¬†49% &quotOther/Support&quot may include outdated contacts</li>
<li><b>Filter out irrelevant:</b>¬†Retail roles (Lacrosse Unlimited) may not be relevant</li>
<li><b>Contact validation:</b>¬†6-12 months old = likely 10-15% have changed roles</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Success Metrics to Track:</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Reply rate by loss reason</li>
<li>Conversion by seniority level</li>
<li>Time-to-re-engagement (from first touch to meeting booked)</li>
<li>Win-back close rate by original loss reason</li>
</ul>
</ol>
<div><b>Why This Works:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Patient approach:</b>¬†Win-backs require trust rebuilding</li>
<li><b>Multi-level engagement:</b>¬†Contacts at all levels need different proof points</li>
<li><b>Shows evolution:</b>¬†Demonstrates you've improved since they left</li>
<li><b>Incentive-driven:</b>¬†Win-back offers have 2-3x higher conversion than cold outreach</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Cross-Campaign Analysis</b></div>
<div><b>Should These Be Sequenced or Run in Parallel?</b></div>
<div><b>Recommendation: Run in Parallel with Staggered Starts</b>¬†<b>Timing:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Week 1:</b>¬†Launch Campaign 2 (Braintrust) - Fastest velocity, cleanest data</li>
<li><b>Week 2:</b>¬†Launch Campaign 1 (Legal) - Requires more prep for multi-threading</li>
<li><b>Week 3:</b>¬†Launch Campaign 3 (Win-back) - Needs historical research first</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Why Parallel?</b><br></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Different audiences:</b>¬†No overlap between campaigns</li>
<li><b>Different buying motions:</b>¬†Each requires unique approach</li>
<li><b>Resource efficiency:</b>¬†Stagger to avoid overwhelming SDR/AE capacity</li>
<li><b>Learning velocity:</b>¬†Insights from fast-moving Campaign 2 inform others</li>
</ol>
<div><b>Recommended Technology Stack</b></div>
<div><b>Essential for Multi-Touch Sequencing:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Mixmax</b>¬†(obviously) for sequences, tracking, templates</li>
<li><b>Video messaging tool</b>¬†(Loom/Vidyard) for Touch 1 in Legal + Win-back</li>
<li><b>Mutual action plan tool</b>¬†(Recapped/Arrows) for multi-threaded Legal campaign</li>
<li><b>Call tracking</b>¬†for measuring phone follow-ups</li>
<li><b>Intent data</b>¬†(if available) to prioritize responders</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Resource Allocation</b></div>
<div><b>Campaign 2 (Braintrust) - Lower Touch:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Can be run primarily by SDR team</li>
<li>Director-level buyers, faster cycle</li>
<li>High automation potential</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Campaign 1 (Legal) - Higher Touch:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Requires AE involvement for C-level outreach</li>
<li>Solutions engineer for technical deep-dives</li>
<li>Industry expert (legal tech) for credibility</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Campaign 3 (Win-back) - Highest Touch:</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li>Executive sponsorship for CRO/VP outreach</li>
<li>CS leader involvement to address previous concerns</li>
<li>AE-led for all opportunities</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Data Quality &amp Hygiene Recommendations</b></div>
<div><b>Legal Campaign Issues:</b></div>
<ul>
<li>&quotLegal Technology Trainier&quot (typo - should be Trainer)</li>
<li>Validate Shareholder/Partner contacts - may need different approach</li>
<li>Some title ambiguity (&quotDirector&quot without clear function)</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Braintrust Campaign:</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Cleanest data</b>¬†- ready to go</li>
<li>Consider asking: &quotWhy so many Director-level but no C-suite?&quot (May indicate company stage/structure)</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Win-Back Campaign:</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>High noise in &quotOther&quot category (49%)</b>¬†- needs filtering</li>
<li>Lacrosse Unlimited retail contacts may not be target ICP</li>
<li>Validate employment: 10-15% likely changed companies in 6-12 months</li>
<li><b>Action item:</b>¬†Run email verification before launch</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Success Metrics by Campaign</b></div>
<div><b>Campaign 1 (Legal Lookalikes):</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Target reply rate:</b>¬†8-12% (C-level brings down average)</li>
<li><b>Target meeting set rate:</b>¬†5-7%</li>
<li><b>Target multi-threaded engagement:</b>¬†15% of accounts with 2+ responders</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Campaign 2 (Braintrust Lookalikes):</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Target reply rate:</b>¬†12-18% (peer-to-peer conversation)</li>
<li><b>Target meeting set rate:</b>¬†8-12%</li>
<li><b>Target demo completion rate:</b>¬†60%+</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Campaign 3 (Win-Back):</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Target reply rate:</b>¬†5-8% (harder to re-engage)</li>
<li><b>Target meeting set rate:</b>¬†3-5%</li>
<li><b>Target reactivation rate:</b>¬†1-3% of list (3-8 reactivated customers)</li>
<li><b>Higher bar:</b>¬†But those who convert have higher LTV (already familiar with product)</li>
</ul>
<div><br></div>
<div><b>Final Recommendations</b></div>
<div><b>Yes, Sequence These with Multi-Faceted Touchpoints:</b></div>
<div><b>Campaign 1 (Legal):</b>¬†Multi-threading is¬†<b>essential</b>¬†- legal buying involves multiple stakeholders. Use 5-touch, 3-persona approach.¬†<b>Campaign 2 (Braintrust):</b>¬†Fast cadence, 4-touch sales-to-sales sequence. High volume allows for A/B testing.¬†<b>Campaign 3 (Win-back):</b>¬†Patient, personalized 6-touch approach with loss-reason segmentation.<b><br></b></div>
<div><b>Do NOT:</b></div>
<ul>
<li>Run all three simultaneously (stagger launches)</li>
<li>Use same messaging across campaigns (each needs unique approach)</li>
<li>Neglect data hygiene (especially Win-back list)</li>
<li>Skip historical research for Win-back campaign</li>
</ul>
<div><b>Critical Success Factors:</b></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Personalization at scale:</b>¬†Use Mixmax variables for company name, pain points, competitor mentions</li>
<li><b>Multi-channel approach:</b>¬†Email + LinkedIn + phone for high-value targets</li>
<li><b>Fast follow-up:</b>¬†Respond to replies within 2 hours</li>
<li><b>Track by persona:</b>¬†Measure success by functional area and seniority</li>
<li><b>Iterate quickly:</b>¬†Campaign 2 results should inform Campaign 1 &amp 3 messaging</li>
</ol>
<div><b>Bottom line:</b>¬†These are three fundamentally different campaigns that each deserve dedicated sequencing strategies. Run in parallel with staggered starts, personalized approaches, and clear success metrics for each.</div>

<div><u>Mixmax AI Persona Builder &amp Messaging Framework</u><br></div>

<div><b>Positioning/Messaging</b></div>
<div><b>Mission/Vision</b></div>
<div><b>Legacy Sales Engagement is dead. AI Sales Execution is here.</b><br></div>
<div>AI killed the spray-and-pray database era. No more buying 500 contacts and blasting them into submission. Today's AI intelligently identifies the right people at the right time‚Äîwhether they're prospects, active opportunities, or existing customers ready to expand. That first touch? Perfected.</div>
<div><b>But then we blow it.</b><br></div>
<div>After that brilliant first interaction, we shove everyone‚Äîprospects, deals, customers‚Äîinto the same broken system: sequences, tasks, activities. More touches, more emails, more calls. The numbers game. We use AI to identify perfect timing, then ignore every signal that comes after.</div>
<div>Here's what's actually happening across your entire revenue org:</div>
<div><b>Your SDR</b> is missing that prospect who went dark (now talking to competitors). <b>Your AE</b> forgot to send the security docs they promised (credibility destroyed). <b>Your AM</b> didn't catch when the champion mentioned &quotbudget concerns&quot on the QBR (renewal at risk). <b>Your AM</b> doesn't know three users just visited your enterprise pricing page (expansion opportunity invisible). Someone forwarded an email to their boss‚Äîcould be a prospect becoming a deal, a deal becoming closed-won, or a customer becoming an advocate‚Äîbut you'll never know.</div>
<div>These signals determine every revenue outcome. <b>And you're blind to all of them.</b><br></div>
<div><b>Enter AI Sales Execution.</b> Mixmax watches every interaction across every channel‚Äîprospecting, selling, onboarding, expanding‚Äîto surface exactly WHO needs attention and WHY. Whether it's an SDR's first touch, an AE's deal progression, or a CSM's renewal at risk. But here's what everyone else misses‚Äîsignals without action are worthless.</div>
<div>Prospect went dark? Win-back email ready. Forgot what you promised? Already sent. Customer mentioned concerns? Follow-up addressing it in drafts. Email forwarded internally? Intros for each new stakeholder ready. Quiet account suddenly active? Strike-while-hot message waiting. Multiple people checking pricing? Personalized outreach for each, ready to execute.</div>
<div><b>The difference between knowing and doing is the difference between noise and revenue.</b><br></div>
<div>This isn't about pipeline stages or customer segments. It's about catching every signal from every interaction with every person who matters to your business. From first touch to renewal and beyond.</div>
<div><b>Stop playing the numbers game. Start executing with intelligence.</b><br></div>

<li><b>Brand Point of View</b>We believe that success in modern sales requires more than just knowing‚Äîit demands doing, instantly and intelligently. Our approach is to empower sellers with AI that identifies exactly who needs attention right now AND executes the perfect response in seconds, ensuring no signal is missed and no momentum is lost. Unlike legacy sales engagement platforms built for the spray-and-pray era, we focus on the critical signals that actually close deals‚Äîthe moments hidden in emails, meetings, and interactions that others ignore‚Äîturning noise into revenue through intelligent execution, not mindless activity.</li>
<li><font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">üéØ</font><b> The Core Formula</b><br><b>Signal + Execution = Sales Excellence</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Signal without execution = Wasted insights (Gong, Chorus)</li>
<li>Execution without signal = Blind activity (Outreach, Salesloft)</li>
<li>Signal + Execution = Focused, effective selling (Mixmax)</li>
</ul>
<li><i>Every feature, message, and decision must reinforce this formula.</i><br></li>
<li><b>The Formula Breakdown</b><br></li>
</ul>

<div><b>Tone of Voice</b></div>
<div><b>Meet ‚ÄúMax‚Äù The Mixmax Voice Formula</b></div>
<div>Max is a seasoned sales professional turned tech innovator. They‚Äôve carried a quota, lost deals to bad tools, and won President‚Äôs Club three times. They‚Äôve been an SDR eating ramen, an AE missing kids‚Äô bedtimes, and a manager trying to help everyone succeed. Now they‚Äôre on a mission to fix what‚Äôs broken in sales.</div>
<div><b>Smart (35%) + Human (30%) + Rebellious (25%) + Playful (10%)</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Smart (The Magician Archetype)</b><br><b>How it sounds</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>‚ÄúHere‚Äôs what the data actually tells us‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúMost people don‚Äôt realize that‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúThe intelligence shows‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
</ul>
<li><b>What it means</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Back claims with data</li>
<li>Provide insights, not just information</li>
<li>Educate without lecturing</li>
<li>Simplify complexity</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Examples</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>‚ÄúYour reps switch tools 30 times per hour. Each switch costs 5-8 minutes. That‚Äôs 40% of their day gone.‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúAI analyzing 50 accounts in parallel beats human intuition every time. Here‚Äôs why‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Human (The Creator Archetype)</b><br><b>How it sounds</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>‚ÄúWe‚Äôve all been there‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúRemember when you‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúIt‚Äôs like when‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
</ul>
<li><b>What it means</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Acknowledge emotions</li>
<li>Share relatable experiences</li>
<li>Use everyday analogies</li>
<li>Be vulnerable when appropriate</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Examples</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>‚ÄúWe get it. Sunday night pipeline reviews are nobody‚Äôs idea of fun.‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúIt‚Äôs like trying to juggle while riding a unicycle. Possible? Yes. Sustainable? No.‚Äù</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Rebellious (The Outlaw Archetype)</b><br><b>How it sounds</b><br></li>

<li>‚ÄúWhile everyone else is‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>
<li>‚ÄúThe dirty secret is‚Ä¶‚Äù</li>

<li>Take stands on issues</li>
<li>Be contrarian when right</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Examples</b><br></li>

<li><b>Playful (The Jester Archetype)</b><br><b>How it sounds</b><br></li>

<li>Never force it</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Examples</b><br></li>

<div><b>The Mixmax Content Commandments</b></div>
<ul>
<li><b>1. Lead with Value, Not Features</b><br><font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚ùå</font> <b>Don‚Äôt:</b> ‚ÄúOur AI-powered signal detection algorithm uses machine learning to‚Ä¶‚Äù <font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚úÖ</font> <b>Do:</b> ‚ÄúStop guessing which customer need attention. Know instantly.‚Äù</li>
<li><b>2. Show, Don‚Äôt Tell</b><br><font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚ùå</font> <b>Don‚Äôt:</b> ‚ÄúMixmax is revolutionary and innovative‚Äù <font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚úÖ</font> <b>Do:</b> ‚ÄúWhile others chase 100 cold leads, Mixmax users close 3 hot deals‚Äù</li>
<li><b>3. Embrace Contrarian Views</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Challenge ‚Äúmore activity = more sales‚Äù</li>
<li>Question ‚Äúbest practices‚Äù that waste time</li>
<li>Offer fresh perspectives on old problems</li>
<li>Stand against conventional wisdom when wrong</li>
</ul>
<li><b>4. Write Like You Talk</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Use contractions (we‚Äôre, you‚Äôll, it‚Äôs)</li>
<li>Start sentences with ‚ÄúAnd‚Äù or ‚ÄúBut‚Äù</li>
<li>Ask rhetorical questions</li>
<li>Use ‚Äúyou‚Äù and ‚Äúyour‚Äù liberally</li>
<li>Short paragraphs (3-4 lines max)</li>
</ul>
<li><b>5. Be Specific, Not Generic</b><br><font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚ùå</font> <b>Don‚Äôt:</b> ‚ÄúSave time on sales tasks‚Äù <font face=".AppleColorEmojiUI">‚úÖ</font> <b>Do:</b> ‚ÄúGet back 2 hours every day from automated follow-ups‚Äù</li>
<li><b>6. Include the Human Element</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Acknowledge the Sunday scaries</li>
<li>Reference the quota pressure</li>
<li>Understand the family trade-offs</li>
<li>Recognize the career ambitions</li>
</ul>
<li><b>7. Make Complex Simple</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Use analogies people understand</li>
<li>Break down AI into outcomes</li>
<li>Avoid technical jargon</li>
<li>Focus on ‚Äúwhat it means for you‚Äù</li>
</ul>
</ul>

<div><b>Product Snapshots</b></div>
<div><b>How The Three Copilots Work Together</b></div>
<ol>
<li><b>Engagement Copilot</b> identifies which deals need attention and recommends the best action</li>
<li><b>Inbox Copilot</b> helps execute that action with perfectly crafted communications</li>
<li><b>Meeting Copilot</b> manages the resulting conversations and follow-ups</li>
<li><b>Intelligent Workflows</b> connects everything automatically in the background</li>
</ol>
<div>The result: Every seller performs like your best seller, working less while achieving more.</div>
<div><b>Engagement Copilot</b></div>
<div><i>Your account strategist that analyzes your entire pipeline and tells you exactly what each prospect needs to move forward. Like having a sales coach watching every account, recommending the perfect next move - whether it's a call, email, or LinkedIn touch - at exactly the right moment.</i><br></div>
<div><b>Core Products Under Engagement Copilot</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Smart Triggers ‚Üí Max Actions</b>Like having a personal assistant who watches all your accounts 24/7 and taps you on the shoulder when something important happens. No more wondering which of your dozens of accounts needs attention - AI tells you exactly which 5 actions matter TODAY.</li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Continuously monitors your accounts and surfaces critical buying signals, engagement patterns, and risk indicators in real-time, then prioritizes exactly what needs your attention right now</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Real-time monitoring of email opens, link clicks, and document views</li>
<li>Risk detection for deals going dark</li>
<li>Opportunity alerts for expansion and upsell</li>
<li>Competitive threat identification</li>
<li>Next best action recommendations</li>
<li>Daily priority list generation</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Missing critical buying signals buried in data</li>
<li>Not knowing which of 50+ deals need attention</li>
<li>Deals slipping through cracks unnoticed</li>
<li>Reactive firefighting instead of proactive engagement</li>
<li>Wasting time on dead deals while hot ones cool</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>25% improvement in close rates</li>
<li>0% missed critical moments</li>
<li>50% faster response to buying signals</li>
<li>100% pipeline coverage</li>
<li>15 minutes to daily clarity (vs. 45 minutes scanning)</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotI used to spend 45 minutes every morning trying to figure out priorities. Now Mixmax shows me the 5 things that matter in 30 seconds. I've closed 40% more deals just from better focus.&quot - Michael Chen, AE at TechStartup Inc.</li>
</ul>
<li><b>AI Sequence Builder ‚Üí Max Builder</b>Pick your target (like &quotEnterprise IT Decision Maker&quot), select your goal, and get a complete 7-touch campaign with emails, LinkedIn messages, and call scripts in 2 minutes. What used to take half your Monday morning now happens before your coffee gets cold.</li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Automatically generates complete multi-touch outreach campaigns tailored to specific personas, industries, and sales objectives using AI that understands what messaging works.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Persona-specific campaign generation</li>
<li>Multi-channel sequence creation (email, LinkedIn, phone)</li>
<li>Industry and role customization</li>
<li>A/B testing variations</li>
<li>Automatic timing optimization</li>
<li>Call script generation</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Hours spent creating campaigns from scratch</li>
<li>Generic sequences that don't resonate</li>
<li>Inconsistent messaging across team</li>
<li>Not knowing what messaging works</li>
<li>Manual campaign creation bottlenecks</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Sequence creation time: 2 minutes (vs. 2 hours)</li>
<li>35% higher engagement rates</li>
<li>50% more meetings booked</li>
<li>100% message consistency</li>
<li>5x faster campaign launch</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotWe used to spend every Monday morning building sequences. Now our entire quarterly campaign strategy is done in an hour. Response rates jumped from 8% to 43%.&quot - Sarah Martinez, SDR Manager at GrowthCo</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Smart Personalization ‚Üí Max Tailor (FUTURE)</b>Your AI writing partner that crafts personalized messages for each prospect based on what they actually care about. Instead of the typical &quotspray and pray&quot where only 2-3 people respond out of 100, get more than half to actually engage in conversation.</li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Analyzes prospect data, company news, social activity, and behavioral patterns to create hyper-personalized messages that resonate with each individual recipient's specific situation, challenges, and interests.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>LinkedIn activity and post analysis</li>
<li>Company news and trigger event detection</li>
<li>Role-specific pain point mapping</li>
<li>Industry trend incorporation</li>
<li>Personal interest identification</li>
<li>Dynamic content insertion</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Generic templates getting ignored</li>
<li>Hours spent researching prospects</li>
<li>Low 2-3% response rates</li>
<li>Irrelevant messaging</li>
<li>Lack of personal connection</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Response rates: 3% ‚Üí 52%</li>
<li>Research time: 30 min ‚Üí 30 seconds per prospect</li>
<li>Relevance score: 95% message-fit</li>
<li>Engagement rate: 17x improvement</li>
<li>Reply sentiment: 85% positive</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotSmart Personalization changed the game. We went from spray and pray to precision targeting. Prospects actually thank us for reaching out because the messages are so relevant to their actual challenges.&quot - Mike Reynolds, Head of Sales Development</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Smart Engagement ‚Üí Max Engage (FUTURE)</b><br><i>Your engagement evolves dynamically with customer behavior. When a prospect opens your email 5 times after a week of silence, Smart Engagement automatically creates a call task. It reads digital body language and triggers the right action at the perfect moment.</i><br></li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Monitors all prospect interactions in real-time, detects behavioral patterns that indicate buying intent or risk, then automatically triggers the appropriate next action - whether that's a call task, a different message type, or an internal alert.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Real-time behavioral pattern detection</li>
<li>Dynamic action triggering based on engagement</li>
<li>Multi-signal intelligence (opens, clicks, time spent, frequency)</li>
<li>Automatic task creation and assignment</li>
<li>Channel switching based on engagement level</li>
<li>Escalation workflows for hot prospects</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Missing buying signals hidden in behavior</li>
<li>Static sequences that don't adapt</li>
<li>Not knowing when to switch from email to call</li>
<li>Delayed response to engaged prospects</li>
<li>One-size-fits-all engagement strategies</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>3x faster response to buying signals</li>
<li>45% improvement in contact rates</li>
<li>30% better timing on outreach</li>
<li>60% increase in hot lead conversion</li>
<li>25% reduction in dropped opportunities</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotA prospect opened our proposal 8 times in 2 hours. Smart Engagement immediately flagged it and created a call task. I called right then - they were literally discussing it in a meeting. Closed the deal that day. This happens weekly now.&quot - Jessica Chen, Mid-Market AE</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<div><b>Inbox Copilot</b></div>
<div><i>Your AI email expert that lives in your inbox, writing personalized responses in your voice and style. Turns 2-hour email sessions into 20-minute power sessions while maintaining the personal touch that builds relationships.</i><br></div>
<div><b>Core Products Under Inbox Copilot</b><br></div>
<ul>
<li><b>Smart Compose ‚Üí Max Compose</b><br><i>Type &quotfollow up on pricing&quot and watch AI write the perfect 3-paragraph email in your voice with all the context, next steps, and personal touches. What used to take 15 minutes of wordsmithing now takes 15 seconds.</i><br></li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does:</b>Uses GPT-4 to generate complete, personalized emails from simple prompts while maintaining your unique voice and including all relevant context from previous conversations.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Natural language email generation</li>
<li>Voice and style matching</li>
<li>Context awareness from thread history</li>
<li>Tone adjustment (formal/casual/urgent)</li>
<li>Subject line optimization</li>
<li>Grammar and clarity enhancement</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Writer's block and blank page paralysis</li>
<li>Time spent crafting perfect emails</li>
<li>Inconsistent communication quality</li>
<li>Forgetting important context</li>
<li>Poor subject lines killing open rates</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>75% reduction in email writing time</li>
<li>15 seconds per email (vs. 15 minutes)</li>
<li>45% higher open rates</li>
<li>100% context inclusion</li>
<li>2+ hours saved daily</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotI used to dread email time. Now I process 100 emails in the time it took to write 10. And they're better - more personal, more effective. My response rate tripled.&quot - Jennifer Park, Enterprise AE at DataTech</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Smart Send</b><br><i>Your emails land at the top of their inbox when they're actually checking email, not buried under 50 others. AI learns when each prospect is most likely to open and respond, then sends automatically at that perfect moment.</i><br></li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Analyzes recipient behavior patterns across millions of interactions to determine and automatically execute optimal email delivery timing for maximum engagement.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>Behavioral pattern analysis</li>
<li>Time zone intelligent scheduling</li>
<li>Industry-specific timing optimization</li>

<li>Visual engagement probability graphs</li>
<li>Automatic send scheduling</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Problems It Solves</b><br></li>
<ul>

<li>Wrong timezone sending</li>
<li>Missing prime engagement windows</li>
<li>Weekend/evening sends hurting response</li>
<li>Guessing when to follow up</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Measurable Benefits</b><br></li>
<ul>
<li>67% improvement in open rates</li>
<li>45% better response rates</li>
<li>3x higher engagement</li>
<li>100% timezone accuracy</li>
<li>Zero manual scheduling</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Customer Proof</b>&quotSmart Send changed everything. Our emails now hit inboxes when prospects are actually reading. Open rates went from 20% to 67%. It's like magic.&quot - David Martinez, SDR at TechStartup Inc.</li>
</ul>
<li><b>Smart Follow-ups ‚Üí Max Follow-Ups</b><br><i>Never miss a deal ‚Äì too many deals die because reps don't follow up. Smart Follow-ups acts like an intelligent assistant in your inbox, reading signals from your conversations and ensuring nothing falls through the cracks.</i><br></li>
<ul>
<li><b>What It Does</b>Functions as an autonomous agent that monitors all sent messages for signals like deadlines, requests, or silence, then automatically schedules reminders and applies organization to ensure every conversation moves forward without manual tracking.</li>
<li><b>Key Capabilities</b><br></li>
<ul>

</ul>

</ul>
